<table style="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;border:0;width:100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid">
<td style="width:11%;vertical-align:top;text-align:left"><span style="font-weight:bold">Item&#8201;2.02.</span></td>
<td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left"> <p style=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left">Results of Operations and Financial Condition. </p></td></tr></table> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On February&#160;12, 2025, Cisco Systems, Inc. (&#8220;Cisco&#8221;) reported its results of operations for its fiscal second quarter 2025 ended January&#160;25, 2025. A copy of the press release issued by Cisco concerning the foregoing results is furnished herewith as Exhibit&#160;99.1. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The information contained herein and in the accompanying exhibit shall not be incorporated by reference into any filing of Cisco, whether made before or after the date hereof, regardless of any general incorporation language in such filing, unless expressly incorporated by specific reference to such filing. The information in this report, including the exhibit hereto, shall not be deemed to be &#8220;filed&#8221; for purposes of Section&#160;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended, or otherwise subject to the liabilities of that section or Sections 11 and 12(a)(2) of the Securities Act of 1933, as amended. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The attached exhibit includes <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</span> net income, <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</span> gross margins, <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</span> operating expenses, <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</span> operating income and margin, <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</span> effective tax rates, <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</span> interest and other income (loss), net, and <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</span> net income per share data for the periods presented. It also includes future estimated ranges for gross margin, operating margin, tax provision rate and EPS on a <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</span> basis. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">These <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</span> measures are not in accordance with, or an alternative for, measures prepared in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles, and may be different from <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</span> measures used by other companies. In addition, these <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</span> measures are not based on any comprehensive set of accounting rules or principles. Cisco believes that <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</span> measures have limitations in that they do not reflect all of the amounts associated with Cisco&#8217;s results of operations as determined in accordance with GAAP and that these measures should only be used to evaluate Cisco&#8217;s results of operations in conjunction with the corresponding GAAP measures. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Cisco believes that the presentation of <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</span> measures when shown in conjunction with the corresponding GAAP measures, provides useful information to investors and management regarding financial and business trends relating to its financial condition and its historical and projected results of operations. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For its internal budgeting process, Cisco&#8217;s management uses financial statements that do not include, when applicable, share-based compensation expense, amortization of acquisition-related intangible assets, acquisition-related/divestiture costs, significant asset impairments and restructurings, significant litigation settlements and other contingencies (such as legal and indemnification settlements and the supplier component remediation amounts), Russia-Ukraine war costs, gains and losses on investments, the income tax effects of the foregoing, and significant tax matters. Cisco&#8217;s management also uses the foregoing <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</span> measures, in addition to the corresponding GAAP measures, in reviewing the financial results of Cisco. In prior periods, Cisco has excluded other items that it no longer excludes for purposes of its <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</span> financial measures. From time to time in the future, there may be other items that Cisco may exclude for purposes of its internal budgeting process and in reviewing its financial results. </p>
</div></div>



<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<hr style="color:#999999;height:3px;width:100%;clear:both"/>

<div style="text-align:center"><div style="width:8.5in;text-align:left;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto">
 <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">As described above, Cisco excludes the following items from one or more of its <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</span> measures when applicable: </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><span style="font-style:italic">Share-based compensation expense.</span> These expenses consist primarily of expenses for employee restricted stock and restricted stock units, employee stock options, and employee stock purchase rights, including such expenses associated with acquisitions. Cisco excludes share-based compensation expense from its <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</span> measures primarily because they are <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</span> expenses and Cisco believes that it is useful to investors to understand the impact of share-based compensation to its results of operations. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><span style="font-style:italic">Amortization of acquisition-related intangible assets</span>. Cisco incurs amortization of intangible assets (which may include impairment charges from the write-downs of purchased intangible assets) in connection with acquisitions. Such intangible assets may include purchased intangible assets with finite lives, capitalized in process research and development and goodwill. Cisco excludes these items because Cisco does not believe these expenses are reflective of ongoing operating results in the period incurred. These amounts arise from Cisco&#8217;s prior acquisitions and have no direct correlation to the operation of Cisco&#8217;s business. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><span style="font-style:italic">Acquisition-related/divestiture costs</span>. In connection with its business combinations, Cisco incurs compensation expense, changes to the fair value of contingent consideration, as well as professional fees and other direct expenses such as restructuring activities related to the acquired company. In addition, from time to time Cisco enters into foreign currency transactions related to pending acquisitions, and may incur gains or losses on such transactions. Cisco may also from time to time incur gains or losses from divestitures of a business area as well as professional fees and other direct expenses associated with such transactions. Cisco excludes such compensation expense, changes to the fair value of contingent consideration, fees, other direct expenses, and gains and losses, as they are related to acquisitions and divestitures and have no direct correlation to the operation of Cisco&#8217;s business. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><span style="font-style:italic">Significant asset impairments and restructurings</span>. Cisco from time to time incurs significant asset impairments, restructuring charges, and gains or losses on asset disposals. Cisco excludes these items, when significant, because it does not believe they are reflective of ongoing business and operating results. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><span style="font-style:italic">Significant litigation settlements and other contingencies</span>. Cisco from time to time may incur charges or benefits related to significant litigation settlements and other contingencies. Cisco excludes these charges or benefits, when significant, because it does not believe they are reflective of ongoing business and operating results. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><span style="font-style:italic">Russia-Ukraine war costs</span>. In past periods, in connection with the Russian invasion of Ukraine, Cisco announced its intention to stop business operations in Russia and Belarus. Cisco began an orderly wind-down and exit of its business in Russia and Belarus. Cisco had incurred certain <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-recurring</span> charges related to this exit plan. These charges included <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-recoverability</span> of certain assets, special personnel-related charges in order to support impacted employees (unrelated to ordinary compensation expenses), potential future litigation and other contingencies, and other exit related costs, among others. Cisco excluded these charges because it believed they were not normal and recurring with respect to ongoing business and operating results. These excluded amounts did not include any impacts to revenue. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><span style="font-style:italic">Gains and losses on investments. </span>Cisco excludes gains and losses on our marketable equity investments and our investments in privately held companies, because it does not believe they are reflective of ongoing business and operating results. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><span style="font-style:italic">Income tax effects of the foregoing</span>. This amount is used to present each of the amounts described above on an <span style="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</span> basis consistent with the presentation of <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</span> net income. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><span style="font-style:italic">Significant tax matters. </span>Cisco may incur tax charges or benefits that are (i)&#160;related to prior periods or (ii)&#160;not reflective of its ongoing provision for income taxes. These tax charges or benefits may be the result of events such as changes in tax legislation, court decisions, and/or tax settlements. Cisco excludes these charges or benefits, when significant, because it does not believe they are reflective of ongoing business and operating results. </p>
</div></div>



<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<hr style="color:#999999;height:3px;width:100%;clear:both"/>

<div style="text-align:center"><div style="width:8.5in;text-align:left;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto">
 <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">From time to time in the future, there may be other items that Cisco may exclude if it believes that doing so is consistent with the goal of providing useful information to investors and management. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Cisco will incur share-based compensation expense, amortization of acquisition-related intangible assets, acquisition-related costs, and gains and losses on investments, in future periods. Significant asset impairments, restructurings, significant litigation settlements and other contingencies, and divestiture costs could occur in future periods. Cisco could also be impacted by significant tax matters in future periods. </p>
</div></div>



<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<hr style="color:#999999;height:3px;width:100%;clear:both"/>

guidance range </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:4pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Revenue:</B> $56.0 billion to $56.5 billion </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:4pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Earnings per Share:</B> GAAP: $2.40 to $2.52; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP:</FONT> $3.68 to $3.74
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">SAN JOSE, Calif. &#151; February&nbsp;12, 2025 &#151; Cisco today reported second quarter results for the period ended January&nbsp;25,
2025. Cisco reported second quarter revenue of $14.0&nbsp;billion, net income on a generally accepted accounting principles (GAAP) basis of $2.4&nbsp;billion or $0.61 per share, and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> net income of
$3.8&nbsp;billion or $0.94 per share. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Cisco&#146;s strong quarterly results were driven by accelerating customer demand for our technology&#148;
said Chuck Robbins, chair and CEO of Cisco. &#147;As AI becomes more pervasive, we are well positioned to help our customers scale their network infrastructure, increase their data capacity requirements, and adopt <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">best-in-class</FONT></FONT> AI security.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Q2 was another quarter of solid execution which drove revenue and EPS
above our guidance ranges. Splunk continues to perform in line with our expectations on the top line, and was accretive to Q2 <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> EPS, earlier than we had planned&#148; said Scott Herren, CFO of Cisco.
&#147;Our strong cash flows have led us to increase our annual dividend again this year, as well as our overall share repurchase authorization.&#148; </P>

basis are provided in the tables located in the section entitled &#147;Reconciliations of GAAP to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> Measures.&#148; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Cisco Increases Quarterly Dividend; Stock Repurchase Program Authorization Increased </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Cisco has declared a quarterly dividend of $0.41 per common share, a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1-cent</FONT> increase or up 3% over the previous
quarter&#146;s dividend, to be paid on April&nbsp;23, 2025, to all stockholders of record as of the close of business on April&nbsp;3, 2025. Future dividends will be subject to Board approval. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Cisco&#146;s board of directors has also approved a $15&nbsp;billion increase to the authorization of the stock repurchase program. There is no fixed
termination date for the repurchase program. The remaining authorized fixed amount for stock repurchases including the additional authorization is approximately $17&nbsp;billion. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">2 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Financial Summary </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>All comparative percentages are on a year-over-year basis unless otherwise noted. </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Q2 FY 2025 Highlights </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Revenue &#151; </I></B>Total
revenue was $14.0&nbsp;billion, up 9%, with product revenue up 11% and services revenue up 6%. Excluding the contribution from Splunk, total revenue was down 1%. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Revenue by geographic segment was: Americas up 9%, EMEA up 11%, and APJC up 8%. Product revenue performance reflected growth in Security up 117%,
Observability up 47%, and Collaboration up 1%. Networking was down 3%. Excluding Splunk, Security and Observability grew 4% and 3%, respectively, in the second quarter of fiscal 2025. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Gross Margin &#151;</I></B><I> </I>On a GAAP basis, total gross margin, product gross margin, and services gross margin were 65.1%, 63.7%, and 68.9%,
respectively, as compared with 64.2%, 62.7%, and 68.2%, respectively, in the second quarter of fiscal 2024. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On a
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> basis, total gross margin, product gross margin, and services gross margin were 68.7%, 67.7%, and 71.6%, respectively, as compared with 66.7%, 65.2%, and 70.5%, respectively, in the second quarter of
fiscal 2024. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Total gross margins by geographic segment were: 67.6% for the Americas, 71.3% for EMEA and 68.3% for APJC. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Operating Expenses &#151;</I></B><B> </B>On a GAAP basis, operating expenses were $6.0&nbsp;billion, up 17%, and were 42.9% of revenue. <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> operating expenses were $4.8&nbsp;billion, up 10%, and were 34.0% of revenue. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Operating Income
&#151;</I></B> GAAP operating income was $3.1&nbsp;billion, up 1%, with GAAP operating margin of 22.3%. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> operating income was $4.9&nbsp;billion, up 15%, with
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> operating margin at 34.7%. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Provision for Income Taxes &#151;</I></B> The GAAP tax provision rate
was 15.9%. The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> tax provision rate was 19.0%. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Net Income and EPS &#151;</I></B> On a GAAP basis,
net income was $2.4&nbsp;billion, a decrease of 8%, and EPS was $0.61, a decrease of 6%. On a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> basis, net income was $3.8&nbsp;billion, an increase of 6%, and EPS was $0.94, an increase of 8%. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Cash Flow from Operating Activities &#151;</I></B> $2.2&nbsp;billion for the second quarter of fiscal 2025, an increase of 177%, compared with
$0.8&nbsp;billion for the second quarter of fiscal 2024. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Balance Sheet and Other Financial Highlights </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Cash and Cash Equivalents and Investments &#151; </I></B>$16.9&nbsp;billion at the end of the second quarter of fiscal 2025, compared with
$17.9&nbsp;billion at the end of fiscal 2024. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Remaining Performance Obligations (RPO)</I></B> <B><I>&#151;</I></B> $41.3&nbsp;billion, up 16% in
total, with 51% of this amount to be recognized as revenue over the next 12 months. Product RPO up 25% and services RPO up 8%. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Deferred Revenue
&#151; </I></B>$27.8&nbsp;billion, up 8% in total, with deferred product revenue up 12%. Deferred services revenue up 4%. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Capital Allocation &#151;
</I></B>In the second quarter of fiscal 2025, we returned $2.8&nbsp;billion to stockholders through share buybacks and dividends. We declared and paid a cash dividend of $0.40 per common share, or $1.6&nbsp;billion, and repurchased approximately
21&nbsp;million shares of common stock under our stock repurchase program at an average price of $58.58 per share for an aggregate purchase price of $1.2&nbsp;billion. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Acquisitions </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In the second quarter of fiscal 2025, we
closed the acquisition of Deeper Insights AI Ltd., a privately held AI services company. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">3 </P>

</DIV></Center>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Excluding Splunk, Security and Observability grew 4% and 3% year over year, respectively, in the second quarter of fiscal

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>CISCO SYSTEMS, INC. </B></P>

their data capacity requirements, and adopt <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">best-in-class</FONT></FONT> AI security) and the future financial performance of Cisco (including the guidance for Q3 FY 2025 and full year
FY 2025) that involve risks and uncertainties. Readers are cautioned that these forward-looking statements are only predictions and may differ materially from actual future events or results due to a variety of factors, including: business and
economic conditions and growth trends in the networking industry, our customer markets and various geographic regions; global economic conditions and uncertainties in the geopolitical environment; our development and use of artificial intelligence;
overall information technology spending; the growth and evolution of the Internet and levels of capital spending on Internet-based systems; variations in customer demand for products and services, including sales to the service provider market,
cloud, enterprise and other customer markets; the return on our investments in certain key priority areas, and in certain geographical locations, as well as maintaining leadership in Networking and services; the timing of orders and manufacturing
and customer lead times; supply constraints; changes in customer order patterns or customer mix; insufficient, excess or obsolete inventory; variability of component costs; variations in sales channels, product costs or mix of products sold; our
ability to successfully acquire businesses and technologies and to successfully integrate and operate these acquired businesses and technologies; our ability to achieve expected benefits of our partnerships; increased competition in our product and
services markets, including the data center market; dependence on the introduction and market acceptance of new product offerings and standards; rapid technological and market change; manufacturing and sourcing risks; product defects and returns;
litigation involving patents, other intellectual property, antitrust, stockholder and other matters, and governmental investigations; our ability to achieve the benefits of restructurings and possible changes in the size and timing of related
charges; cyber attacks, data breaches or other incidents; vulnerabilities and critical security defects; our ability to protect personal data; evolving regulatory uncertainty; terrorism; natural catastrophic events (including as a result of global
climate change); any pandemic or epidemic; our ability to achieve the benefits anticipated from our investments in sales, engineering, service, marketing and manufacturing activities; our ability to recruit and retain key personnel; our ability to
manage financial risk, and to manage expenses during economic downturns; risks related to the global nature of our operations, including our operations in emerging markets; currency fluctuations and other international factors; changes in provision
for income taxes, including changes in tax laws and regulations or adverse outcomes resulting from examinations of our income tax returns; potential volatility in operating results; and other factors listed in Cisco&#146;s most recent reports on

certain points during the year. Such information speaks only as of the date of this release. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This release includes
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> net income, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> gross margins, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> operating expenses, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Cisco believes that the presentation of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures when shown
in conjunction with the corresponding GAAP measures, provides useful information to investors and management regarding financial and business trends relating to its financial condition and its historical and projected results of operations. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For its internal budgeting process, Cisco&#146;s management uses financial statements that do not include, when applicable, share-based compensation expense,
amortization of acquisition-related intangible assets, acquisition/divestiture-related costs, significant asset impairments and restructurings, significant litigation settlements and other contingencies, Russia-Ukraine war costs, gains and losses on
investments, the income tax effects of the foregoing and significant tax matters. Cisco&#146;s management also uses the foregoing <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures, in addition to the corresponding GAAP measures, in reviewing
the financial results of Cisco. In prior periods, Cisco has excluded other items that it no longer excludes for purposes of its <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures. From time to time in the future there may be other
items that Cisco may exclude for purposes of its internal budgeting process and in reviewing its financial results. For additional information on the items excluded by Cisco from one or more of its <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT>
financial measures, refer to the Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">8-K</FONT> regarding this release furnished today to the Securities and Exchange Commission. </P>
